       <section class="l-content-width section section--bordered"> 
        <div class="section__description"> 
         <h2 class="section__headline visuallyhidden">Description</h2> 
         <div class="l-row"> 
          <div class="we-truncate we-truncate--multi-line we-truncate--interactive  l-column small-12 medium-9 large-8" dir aria-label> 
           <p dir="false" data-test-bidi>Google Pay is a safe, simple, and helpful way to manage your money, giving you a clearer picture of your spending and savings: <br>- Pay at your favorite stores and online<br>- Send and receive money from friends, family or split expenses with a group<br>- Connect with your favorite businesses and discover new ones<br>- Save money &amp; earn rewards for everyday purchases<br>- Understand your spending &amp; get a clearer view of your finances<br><br>MAKE PAYMENTS FAST &amp; EASY<br><br>Send &amp; receive money<br>+ Transfer money easily to friends &amp; family safely<br>+ Create a group to send and receive money for things like trips, dinner, bills, rent, and more. Google Pay will even help you do the math on who owes what. <br>+ Money transfers are instant and free with your Google Pay balance. There are no fees if you use ACH to withdraw funds<br><br>Your shared payments stay private<br>+ When you send a payment with Google Pay, it stays between you and your friends. Only the people involved in the transaction see it. <br><br>Connect with your favorite businesses and discover new ones<br>+ See businesses where you’ve used Google Pay when you open the app. Get quick access to your transactions, loyalty cards, and activate offers.<br><br>Discover nearby restaurants and order a meal<br>+ No need to switch between different delivery apps. Explore places to eat, see menus, and order a meal for pickup or delivery with just a few taps. <br><br>Fuel your next adventure <br>+ Find nearby gas stations, see prices, and pay for fuel right from the app. Google Pay will help you enroll in rewards programs and automatically apply rewards at the pump so you’ll always get the best deal. <br><br>Shop online<br>+ Use Google Pay to checkout quickly and securely when you shop on websites and apps.<br><br>ORGANIZE AND UNDERSTAND YOUR MONEY<br><br>Manage your money<br>+ See the total balance from all of your accounts in one payment app, so you’ll always know exactly what’s coming in and what’s going out.<br>+ Get reminders about upcoming bill payments.<br><br>Stay on top of your spending <br>+ Get weekly summaries, track trends over time, and see what you’ve spent at every business.<br><br>All your transactions, all together<br>+ With your permission, you can see activity from accounts you've linked. Import receipts from Gmail and Google Photos and then simply search for any of them. <br><br>SAVE AND GROW YOUR MONEY<br><br>Earn rewards you can use right away<br>+ Get cashback for things like paying and referring friends. Any money you receive will go straight to your balance so you can use it instantly.<br><br>Double down on cashback<br>+ Activate offers and get cashback for redeeming them – whether you use Google Pay or your plastic card. Better yet: get twice the rewards when you redeem with a cashback credit card.<br><br>Loyalty made easy <br>+ No more sign-up forms or punch cards. Easily enroll in loyalty and rewards programs from the app, then let Google Pay apply points and perks automatically. <br><br>SECURITY &amp; CONTROL<br><br>Authentication for every payment<br>+ You'll need to use your fingerprint, pattern, PIN, or face to verify your identity each time you open the app or make a payment — only you can pay or send money<br><br>Keeping your private information safe<br>+ Try out a more personalized experience to see the most relevant offers from stores and get recommendations for ways to save. Turn it on or off at any time.<br>+ Manage and control personalization and other privacy settings like location preferences and contact syncing from settings<br><br>___________________________<br><br>Features available in India: Make UPI transfers or do mobile recharges, bills and payments to businesses with your bank account with Google Pay. To find out more about Google Pay in India, please visit pay.google.com/intl/en_in/about/<br></p> <!---->
          </div>

           <div class="we-customer-review__header we-customer-review__header--user"> <span class="we-truncate we-truncate--single-line  we-customer-review__user" dir="ltr" aria-label> Musical Barbie </span> <span class="we-customer-review__separator">, </span> <time data-test-customer-review-date datetime="2021-05-11T17:51:37.000Z" aria-label="May 11, 2021" class="we-customer-review__date">05/11/2021</time> 
           </div> 
           <h3 class="we-truncate we-truncate--single-line  we-customer-review__title" dir="ltr" aria-label id="we-customer-review-336092"> Beware! New App is Horrible! </h3> 
           <blockquote class="we-truncate we-truncate--multi-line we-truncate--interactive  we-customer-review__body" dir aria-label> 
            <p dir="false" data-test-bidi>I will be deleting this app immediately! It’s so disappointing to have an app that you love and then go to use it one day only to discover everything you loved about it has changed. Typically, I like updates. This one, however, is horribly unnecessarily complicated. Plus, the new “update” includes being forced to pay a fee for instant deposit when using a debit card. Really Google? I HAVE to pay $15 to transfer $1000 out of my Google ACCT to my bank account if I’m using my debit card? But if I want to use my bank, it will take “up to” 5 days. No worries. I’ll wait. The absolute worst new update I discovered was when I tried to send money from one of my other accounts. I use my Google account to put money aside for my son. Essentially, a temporary saving. Anyway, I go to send money using my other account and was denied access to my own accounts. The message indicated that I HAD to use the money in my Google account before I would be allowed to send money from my other account. Wrap your mind around that. You’re being told that you cannot use your other accounts until you use all the money in your Google account. Unbelievably horrible. Not sure what Goggle was thinking, other than greed. I’ll be going back to Cash App. At least they give you an option to do instant deposit using your debit card. Extremely disappointed.</p> <!---->
           </blockquote> <!---->
          </div>

           </figure> 
           <div class="we-customer-review__header we-customer-review__header--user"> <span class="we-truncate we-truncate--single-line  we-customer-review__user" dir="ltr" aria-label> HHHHHH reviews i guess </span> <span class="we-customer-review__separator">, </span> <time data-test-customer-review-date datetime="2020-12-21T04:49:03.000Z" aria-label="December 20, 2020" class="we-customer-review__date">12/20/2020</time> 
           </div> 
           <h3 class="we-truncate we-truncate--single-line  we-customer-review__title" dir="ltr" aria-label id="we-customer-review-336093"> Confusing App and Will Not Let Me Change My Legal Name </h3> 
           <blockquote class="we-truncate we-truncate--multi-line we-truncate--interactive  we-customer-review__body" dir aria-label> 
            <p dir="false" data-test-bidi>This app is far more convoluted and confusing than I would have thought, to the point that I had to have somebody hold my hand and walk me thru the entire process of setting it up and learning how to use it. I’m 24, I was raised in the age of smart phones, this shouldn't be that difficult for me. But beyond that, when I tried to look at my personal info, it showed my legal name as something completely different from my own, and is locked, making it so I can’t change it. Which is INCREDIBLY STUPID if you ask me bc, even ignoring the fact that it just has me wrong??? People change their names!! Legally!!!! They realize their gender is wrong or they get married or divorced or something! And change their name! But you can’t do that here!! Also, while I realize that most payment apps charge you to remove your money, finding out from other reviews that they didn’t used to have that feature infuriates me even more than it did when i saw the fact they were going to charge me. <br><br>All in all, its a one star from me, bc I just can’t figure it out despite growing up w technology, the movement of capitalism to where every single thing you use tries to charge you infuriates me, and the fact that they LITERALLY gave me the WRONG NAME and WILL NOT let me change it.</p> <!---->
           </blockquote> <!---->
